country_event = { 				
	id = 53112
	
	is_triggered_only  = yes
	
	title = "Factories lost!"
	desc = "Enemies captured our precious factories!"
	picture = "EVT53112"

	trigger = {
		THIS = {
			war = yes
			or = {
				any_owned_province  = {
					is_core = THIS
					not = { controlled_by = THIS }
                    controller = { war_with = THIS }
                    not = { has_province_flag = double_core }
					has_province_flag = automotive_factory_1
					not = { has_province_flag = automotive_factory_1_captured }
				}
				any_owned_province  = {
					is_core = THIS
					not = { controlled_by = THIS }
                    controller = { war_with = THIS }
                    not = { has_province_flag = double_core }
					has_province_flag = automotive_factory_2
					not = { has_province_flag = automotive_factory_2_captured }
				}
				any_owned_province  = {
					is_core = THIS
					not = { controlled_by = THIS }
                    controller = { war_with = THIS }
                    not = { has_province_flag = double_core }
					has_province_flag = automotive_factory_3
					not = { has_province_flag = automotive_factory_3_captured }
				}
				any_owned_province  = {
					is_core = THIS
					not = { controlled_by = THIS }
                    controller = { war_with = THIS }
                    not = { has_province_flag = double_core }
					has_province_flag = automotive_factory_4
					not = { has_province_flag = automotive_factory_4_captured }
				}
				any_owned_province  = {
					is_core = THIS
					not = { controlled_by = THIS }
                    controller = { war_with = THIS }
                    not = { has_province_flag = double_core }
					has_province_flag = automotive_factory_5
					not = { has_province_flag = automotive_factory_5_captured }
				}
				any_owned_province  = {
					is_core = THIS
					not = { controlled_by = THIS }
                    controller = { war_with = THIS }
                    not = { has_province_flag = double_core }
					has_province_flag = automotive_factory_6
					not = { has_province_flag = automotive_factory_6_captured }

			war = yes

				any_owned_province  = {
